### [149] [CGGS: Consistency-Augmented Geometric Gaussian Splatting for Ego-centric 3D Scene Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03819)
*Zhenyu Sun,Xiaohan Zhang,Qi Liu,Huan Wang*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: CGGS是一个文本到3D的框架，通过自中心生成器（基于一致性增强的多视图潜在扩散模型）、布局装饰器（光流与点跟踪估计深度生成点云）和几何精炼器（基于互信息深度损失与分层优化的3D高斯重建）三大模块，解决自中心3D场景生成中视角重叠有限、几何失真等问题，在文本驱动的3D场景生成中优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自中心3D场景生成面临视角重叠有限、个体视角对场景解释的主导影响等挑战，导致难以生成视角一致且语义对齐的视觉内容，以及构建准确的几何结构。

Method: 提出CGGS框架，包含三个模块：1）自中心生成器（Ego-centric Generator）：通过一致性增强损失微调多视图潜在扩散模型，生成与文本描述对齐的一致高保真2D内容；2）布局装饰器（Layout Decorator）：利用光流和点跟踪对应关系估计深度，从自中心2D先验生成密集点云作为粗略布局；3）几何精炼器（Geometric Refiner）：基于熵的互信息深度损失（MID）结合分层优化方案，增强3D高斯重建的视觉质量和几何结构。

Result: 综合实验表明，CGGS在生成连贯且准确的文本驱动3D场景方面优于先前方法。

Conclusion: CGGS通过自中心生成器、布局装饰器和几何精炼器三个模块的协同设计，有效解决了自中心3D场景生成中的几何失真和视角一致性问题，在文本驱动3D场景生成任务上取得了更优的性能。

Abstract: Challenges remain in ego-centric 3D scene generation due to limited view overlap and the dominant influence of individual perspectives on scene interpretation. These factors hinder the creation of viewpoint-consistent and semantically aligned visual content, as well as the construction of accurate geometric structures. In this paper, we propose CGGS, a text-to-3D framework aiming to enhance 3D-content-awareness and address geometric distortions in ego-centric scene generation. Firstly, the Ego-centric Generator is proposed by fine-tuning a Multi-View Latent Diffusion Model with consistency-augmented loss to generate consistent, high-fidelity 2D content aligned with textual descriptions. Then, Layout Decorator leverages optical flow and point-track correspondence to estimate depth, therefore producing dense point clouds as coarse layouts from the ego-centric 2D priors. Building on this initialization, Geometric Refiner is proposed to enhance 3D Gaussian reconstruction via an entropy-based Mutual Information Depth Loss (MID) combined with a hierarchical optimization scheme for improving visual quality and geometric structure. Comprehensive experiments demonstrate that \textcolor{softred}{CGGS} outperforms previous methods in generating coherent and accurate text-driven 3D scenes. Project page: https://cggs-26.github.io/cggs26/.

</details>

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于软件光栅化的延迟渲染管线，用于实时渲染基于发丝的头发，通过延迟着色、发丝过滤与重建以及LOD方案，在单样本每像素下实现高效、可扩展且兼容性强的远场头发渲染。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于发丝的发型渲染方法通常局限于高端硬件，仅用于少数主角角色；而基于头发网格的渲染虽高效但存在性能瓶颈。本文旨在解决这些问题，提升渲染性能与硬件兼容性。

Method: 采用软件光栅化方法，结合延迟着色、发丝过滤与重建步骤，在单样本每像素下实现高效渲染；并引入基于视距和屏幕空间覆盖的LOD方案，动态调整头发表示与着色复杂度。

Result: 所提方法在减少计算开销的同时保持视觉保真度，且仅需最低限度的硬件支持，实现了效率、灵活性、可扩展性与广泛硬件兼容性的结合。

Conclusion: 据我们所知，这是首个实现效率、灵活性、可扩展性与广泛硬件兼容性相结合的发丝头发实时渲染方法。

Abstract: In this work we propose an efficient deferred software rasterization pipeline for real-time rendering of strand-based hair using hair meshes. Hair plays a crucial role in creating expressive 3D characters, yet strand-based approaches are often restricted to high-end hardware and typically applied to only a small number of hero characters. Hair meshes have proven to be an efficient representation capable of handling a wide variety of groom styles, but existing mesh shader-based implementations still suffer from significant bottlenecks. In this work, we address these limitations with a software rasterization approach that improves performance and compatibility. Our method enables efficient far-field strand-based hair rendering-even at a single sample per pixel-by combining deferred shading with a strand filtering and reconstruction step, while requiring only minimal hardware support. To further enhance scalability, we introduce a level-of-detail (LOD) scheme that adapts hair representation and shading complexity based on viewing distance and screen-space coverage, reducing computational cost further while preserving visual fidelity. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first approach to achieve this combination of efficiency, flexibility, scalability, and broad hardware compatibility.

Abstract: This state-of-the-art report provides an overview of controllable 3D human avatar creation. To limit the scope, we focus on the prior learning and avatar creation stages. We define current avatar representations and introduce a taxonomy that categorizes existing work along multiple axes, including body regions and employed priors. We review methods for full-body and head avatars, as well as layered representations that decompose the body into components such as hands, hair, and garments. Finally, we outline common underlying principles, reference key literature for newcomers, and discuss open challenges and future research directions.

### [152] [SceneFrom3D: Geometry-Conditioned Outdoor 3D Scene Generation via View Scheduling with Object-Level Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04540)
*Geonung Kim,Jeongeun Park,Nuri Ryu,Di Liu,Sunghyun Cho*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: SceneFrom3D通过自动视角调度（有向生成图）和对象级条件控制，解决了室外大场景3D生成中的视角调度瓶颈，实现了最优的几何条件约束室外3D场景生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有几何条件3D场景生成方法普遍采用三阶段设计（定义视角调度→合成多视角观测→重建3D表示），但对于室外大尺度、非结构化和无边界几何场景，视角调度成为主要瓶颈，难以获得既能充分覆盖又能支持稳定生成的视角。

Method: SceneFrom3D提出了一种自动视角调度框架，通过构建有向生成图来组织生成过程：节点代表锚定视角，边代表插值轨迹，定义了哪些视角需要合成、哪些视角对需要插值以及生成的顺序。此外，通过对象级条件控制提升可控性，为每个对象分配身份图像用于外观引导，以及几何一致性参数用于区域级几何约束控制。

Result: 实验表明SceneFrom3D在几何条件约束的室外3D场景生成上达到最优水平，生成高质量场景，并实现了可控的对象外观和几何一致性。

Conclusion: SceneFrom3D在几何条件约束的室外3D场景生成任务上达到了最优性能，能够生成高质量场景并支持可控的对象外观和几何一致性。

Abstract: Geometry-conditioned 3D scene generation enables the creation of 3D environments from user-provided geometry, offering direct control over scene structure and object layout. To generate such 3D scenes, current methods commonly adopt a three-stage design that first defines a view schedule, then synthesizes multi-view observations along the scheduled views, and finally reconstructs a 3D representation from the generated images. However, defining the view schedule becomes a major bottleneck for outdoor scenes, where large, unstructured, and unbounded geometry makes it difficult to obtain views that provide sufficient coverage while supporting stable generation. To address this bottleneck, we present SceneFrom3D, a framework that automatically schedules views from outdoor input geometries. SceneFrom3D constructs a directed generation graph whose nodes represent anchor views and whose edges represent interpolation trajectories, defining which views to synthesize, which view pairs to interpolate, and in which order generation should proceed. Beyond automatic view scheduling, SceneFrom3D further improves controllability through object-level conditioning, assigning each object an identity image for appearance guidance and a geometry-adherence parameter for region-wise control over the input geometry. Experiments demonstrate that SceneFrom3D achieves state-of-the-art geometry-conditioned outdoor 3D scene generation, producing high-quality scenes with controllable object appearance and geometry adherence.

</details>


### [153] [StructuredEdit: Constraint-Aware Graphic Design Editing via Differentiable Parameter Propagation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04612)
*Veeramanohar Avudaiappan,Ritwik Murali*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文提出StructuredEdit，一种将设计编辑重构为参数操作而非像素生成的管线。核心贡献是可微参数传播（DPP）训练方法，通过轻量级可微光栅化器反向传播像素级约束违规，将硬设计约束嵌入视觉语言模型微调。系统在约束满足率上达到89%（GPT-4V仅52%），匹配元素IoU 0.82，字体准确率76%，用户研究中编辑时间降低33%，修正迭代减少44%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前视觉语言模型在设计编辑任务中基于像素操作，约束满足率仅52%，难以满足专业工作流对可靠性的要求。

Method: 提出StructuredEdit管线，核心是Differentiable Parameter Propagation (DPP)训练方法，通过可微光栅化器将像素级约束违规反向传播，将硬设计约束嵌入VLM微调；采用混合候选-过滤管线生成12.5万个验证后的编辑三元组。

Result: 约束满足率89% (vs GPT-4V 52%)，匹配元素IoU 0.82，前100种设计字体中Top-1准确率76%；用户研究(N=35)显示编辑时间降低33%，修正迭代减少44%。

Conclusion: 将设计编辑从像素生成重构为参数操作能显著提升约束满足率和编辑效率，为专业级自动化设计编辑提供了可靠方案。

Abstract: Graphic design editing requires precise manipulation of typography, layout, and visual hierarchy under strict design constraints. Following the introduction of large language models, organizations have increasingly promoted vision-language models to enhance productivity. However, current models operate on pixels and achieve only 52% constraint satisfaction on structured design edits, thereby limiting their reliability for professional workflows. We present StructuredEdit, a pipeline that reframes design editing as parameter manipulation rather than pixel generation. Our core technical contribution is Differentiable Parameter Propagation (DPP), a training method that embeds hard design constraints into vision-language model fine-tuning by backpropagating pixel-level constraint violations through a lightweight differentiable rasterizer. A hybrid candidate-and-filter pipeline produces 125k validated edit triplets. The resulting system reaches 89% constraint satisfaction versus 52% for GPT-4V, 0.82 matched-element Intersection over Union, and 76% top-1 font accuracy over the 100 most-frequent design typefaces. In a user study (N=35), editing time drops 33% and correction iterations drop 44% relative to a GPT-4V baseline.

### [154] [Physics-Based Simulation of Contact-Induced Facial Wrinkling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04768)

Result: 在合成示例上评估方法，并与真实视频 footage 对比，结果表明所提出的皮肤模型能够在瞬态接触过程中产生时间连贯且视觉真实的皱纹模式。

Abstract: Facial skin dynamics are inherently challenging to simulate due to a combination of geometric, material, and anatomical complexities. Human skin is a nonlinear layered material with spatially heterogeneous attachments to the underlying tissues. During contact events, localized compression and shear induce mechanical instabilities, leading to fine-scale wrinkling patterns governed by a delicate interplay of geometry, boundary conditions, and through-the-thickness stresses. We present a finite element framework to simulate contact-induced wrinkling of facial skin. We model skin as a viscoelastic material with time-dependent relaxation that governs the rate, persistence, and damping of wrinkle formation. We employ high-order prismatic solid-shell elements to resolve through-thickness stresses and high-frequency deformation modes. Central to our approach, we introduce a continuum-based formulation of skin ligaments to model heterogeneous skin attachments and provide anatomically inspired mobility constraints. These skin ligaments control the formation and appearance of facial wrinkles by modulating their amplitude, wavelength, and spatial distribution. We evaluate our method on a set of synthetic examples and compare simulations with real-world footage. These results demonstrate that our skin model produces temporally coherent and visually realistic wrinkle patterns during transient contact.

### [155] [Glare Mitigation using a Differentiable Unified Glare Rating](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04796)
*Linas Beresna,Eugene Fiume*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种连续、完全可微的CIE统一眩光评级（UGR）代理函数，通过可微分光学散射模拟人眼点扩散函数（PSF）修复评估掩膜，并用可调Sigmoid边界替代离散UGR阶跃函数，实现了从心理物理测量到场景参数的平滑梯度流动，从而在三个辐射度量域（微几何粗糙化、折射率优化、发射器遮罩）中系统性地减少眩光。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统CIE UGR依赖严格的二值阈值，与基于梯度的平滑反向渲染不兼容，无法将眩光这一关键视觉舒适度指标融入可微光学传输优化框架中进行物理逆向设计。

Result: 将被动感知评估转化为主动损失景观，在复杂全局光照环境中实现了对眩光的系统性减少，验证了框架在三个辐射度量域中的有效性。

Abstract: Recent research in differentiable light transport extends the utility of computer graphics algorithms beyond traditional image generation, offering powerful tools for physical inverse design. In architectural and automotive applications, visual discomfort from glare is a critical design rating, traditionally quantified by the discrete CIE Unified Glare Rating (UGR). The standard UGR formulation relies on strict binary thresholds, making it fundamentally incompatible with smooth gradient-based inverse rendering. In this paper, we introduce a continuous, fully differentiable proxy for UGR. To resolve the severe optimisation instabilities caused by Monte Carlo variance at low sample densities, we introduce a differentiable optical scattering pass that simulates the Point Spread Function (PSF) of the human eye to heal fractured evaluation masks. We replace the discrete UGR step function with a tunable sigmoid boundary, enabling gradients to flow smoothly from the psychophysical measure back to the physical scene parameters. We deploy this differentiable framework to systematically reduce glare across three radiometric domains: surface-side microgeometry roughening, boundary-side index of refraction (IOR) optimisation, and source-side emitter gobo masking. By transforming a passive perceptual evaluation into an active loss landscape, our framework provides a robust, physics-based pipeline for optimizing visual comfort in complex global illumination environments.

### [156] [The Binomial Channel: On Capacity, Optimal Inputs, and Beta-Binomial Approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02683)
*Antonino Favano,Mohammadamin Baniasadi,Ian Zieder,Luca Barletta,Alex Dytso*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究了输入字母表为连续区间[0,1]、输出字母表为有限集{0,...,n}的二项信道。证明了容量达到输入分布是离散的、唯一的、关于1/2对称且包含端点0和1，给出了支撑点概率质量的约束和界限，将支撑集大小的Witsenhausen型上界从O(n)改进到O(n/2)，推导了容量的显式非渐近上下界（C(n)=1/2 log(nπ/2e)+o(1)），并证明了支撑集大小的下界为Ω(√(n log log n))。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二项信道是典型的连续输入-有限输出信道，由于输入连续而输出有限，不同输入分布可能诱导相同输出分布，导致最优输入的唯一性和支撑性质不能由严格凹性直接得出。本文旨在建立容量达到输入分布的结构性质，并精确刻画信道容量和最优输入分布的支撑大小。

Method: 利用信息论和概率论方法：通过对称性分析、Witsenhausen技巧改进支撑集上界；采用Beta(1/2,1/2)参考输入诱导Beta-二项输出分布获得下界；利用极小极大冗余构造获得上界；通过相对熵和χ²散度分析输出分布的渐近最优性；结合有限混合逼近下界证明支撑集大小的Ω(√(n log log n))下界。

Result: 建立了容量达到输入分布的离散性、唯一性、对称性和端点包含性；将支撑集上界从O(n)改进到O(n/2)；得到容量C(n)=1/2 log(nπ/2e)+o(1)的显式非渐近上下界；证明了Beta-二项输出在相对熵和χ²散度下渐近最优；证明了支撑集大小的下界为Ω(√(n log log n))。

Conclusion: 本文完整刻画了二项信道的容量和最优输入分布的结构性质，包括支撑大小的上下界改进和容量的精确渐近表达式，为连续输入-有限输出信道的容量分析提供了重要理论框架。

Abstract: We study the binomial channel with input alphabet $[0,1]$ and output alphabet ${0,\ldots,n}$. We investigate its capacity and the structure of the capacity-achieving input and output distributions. Since the output alphabet is finite whereas the input alphabet is continuous, different input distributions may induce the same output distribution; hence, uniqueness and support properties of optimal inputs do not follow from strict concavity arguments. We first establish structural properties of the capacity-achieving input distribution. In particular, we show that it is discrete, unique, symmetric around $1/2$, and contains the endpoints ${0,1}$ in its support. We also derive location constraints and bounds on the probability masses of support points, and improve the Witsenhausen-type upper bound on the support size from order $n$ to order $n/2$. We derive explicit nonasymptotic upper and lower bounds on the capacity $C(n)$. These bounds imply $C(n)=\frac{1}{2}\log\frac{nπ}{2e}+o(1).$ The lower bound is obtained by evaluating the mutual information at the reference input $X_r\sim \mathrm{Beta}(1/2,1/2)$, which induces a beta-binomial output distribution, while the upper bound follows from a minimax redundancy construction. Finally, we prove an improved lower bound on the support size of the capacity-achieving input distribution. We show that the beta-binomial output induced by $X_r$ is asymptotically optimal and close to the capacity-achieving output distribution in relative entropy and $χ^2$ divergence. We also prove a finite-mixture approximation lower bound showing that the beta-binomial output cannot be approximated too accurately by binomial mixtures with few components. Combining these results yields a support-size lower bound of order $Ω(\sqrt{n\log\log n})$, with explicit constants. Numerical results illustrate the capacity bounds and optimal input distribution.

</details>


### [157] [Cramér-Rao Bound Optimization for Massive MIMO DFRC Systems with 1-Bit DACs and ADCs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02878)
*Chenfei Huang,Mingjie Shao,Ya-Feng Liu*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文针对配备1-bit DAC/ADC的大规模MIMO系统，研究了双功能雷达通信(DFRC)下行链路设计，通过优化发射信号矩阵在满足通信QoS约束下最小化1-bit CRB，提出了一种基于增广拉格朗日方法和谱投影梯度法的非凸优化求解方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模MIMO系统在实际部署中面临高成本和高功耗的挑战，采用1-bit DAC/ADC可显著降低硬件开销和能耗，但会引入严重的量化失真。如何在低精度硬件条件下实现高效的雷达通信一体化设计，是当前研究的重要动机。

Method: 首先建立1-bit CRB最小化优化问题，含符号级建设性干扰(CI)约束；对1-bit Fisher信息进行渐近分析，揭示其非单调性并引入幅度约束；将离散问题转化为连续约束问题，利用ALM和SPG方法（结合非单调线搜索）求解；最后通过局部搜索和切割平面技术进一步优化解的质量。

Result: 大量数值实验验证了所提分析的正确性，表明该方法相比基准方案具有优越的DFRC性能。

Conclusion: 所提出的优化框架能够在1-bit量化条件下有效平衡雷达感知与通信性能，为低精度大规模MIMO系统的DFRC设计提供了可行的技术方案。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the dual-function radar-communication (DFRC) design for massive multiple-input multiple-output (MIMO) systems equipped with 1-bit digital-to-analog converters (DACs) at the transmitter and 1-bit analog-to-digital converters (ADCs) at the receiver, motivated by the need for low-cost and power-efficient implementations of massive MIMO systems. We consider a downlink scenario where the transmit signal matrix is optimized to enhance sensing performance while satisfying communication quality of service (QoS) requirements. Specifically, the objective is to minimize the 1-bit Cramér-Rao bound (CRB) for estimating the azimuth angle of a point-like target under symbol-level constructive interference (CI) constraints. We conduct an asymptotic analysis of the 1-bit Fisher information, revealing its nonmonotonicity with the signal-to-noise ratio (SNR), and introduce amplitude constraints to exclude regions where the objective function value is clearly suboptimal and facilitate convergence to high-quality solutions. The resulting problem is a nonconvex optimization challenge with coupled binary and linear constraints. We transform the discrete problem into a continuous constrained one, characterize its global and local minima, and tackle it via the augmented Lagrangian method (ALM) and a spectral projected gradient (SPG) method combined with nonmonotone line search. The solution is further refined via local search and cutting-plane techniques. Extensive numerical experiments verify our analysis, showing that the proposed approach exhibits promising DFRC performance compared to benchmark schemes.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We ask whether interaction is necessary for order-optimal 1-bit mean estimation over nonparametric finite-moment classes. Adaptive threshold-query protocols achieve the order-optimal 1-bit minimax rate, and the same rate is attainable with general 1-bit queries using only one adaptive transition (i.e., two stages of querying). In the non-adaptive setting, threshold and interval queries are known to be highly suboptimal, but the case of arbitrary non-adaptive quantizers remains unresolved. Can such quantizers match the adaptive rate, yielding an optimal one-shot protocol? Or is the known two-stage estimator stage-optimal, with a single adaptive transition being necessary and sufficient?

### [159] [Diffusion-Based Noise-Adaptive Null-Space Channel Estimation for OFDM Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03348)
*Heqiang Qi,Yirun Chen,Xiangming Meng,Chunxiao Jiang,Sheng Wu,Linling Kuang*

TL;DR: 本文提出DANCE，一种基于扩散模型的OFDM信道估计方法，通过噪声自适应后验校正和条件U-Net去噪器，在稀疏、噪声DMRS观测下实现优于传统方法和现有扩散方法的信道估计性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: OFDM系统中，当DMRS观测稀疏且含噪、DMRS配置随部署场景变化时，精确信道估计仍然具有挑战性。

Method: 将DMRS辅助信道估计建模为稀疏线性逆问题，利用测量算子的值域-零空间分解，通过扩散先验重构零空间分量；引入噪声自适应后验校正，避免将噪声导频作为精确约束；设计专用于复值OFDM信道网格的条件U-Net去噪器，实部和虚部作为独立特征通道，仅沿子载波维度下采样。

Result: 基于5G NR TDL和CDL信道模型的仿真表明，DANCE在不同SNR、DMRS配置、多普勒频移及训练-测试分布不匹配条件下，NMSE一致优于传统估计器和扩散后验采样方法。

Abstract: Accurate channel estimation in orthogonal frequency division multiplexing (OFDM) systems remains challenging when demodulation reference signal (DMRS) observations are sparse and noisy, and when DMRS configurations vary across deployment scenarios. This paper proposes DANCE (Diffusion-based Noise-Adaptive Null-space Channel Estimation), a diffusion-based channel estimator for OFDM systems. We formulate DMRS-aided channel estimation as a sparse linear inverse problem whose measurement operator is induced by the pilot pattern. The resulting range-null space decomposition separates the measurement-constrained range-space component from the unobserved null-space component, which is reconstructed through a learned diffusion prior. To avoid directly imposing noisy pilot samples as exact constraints, DANCE introduces a noise-adaptive posterior correction into the reverse diffusion process. The correction coefficient and the residual sampling variance are jointly calibrated according to the observation noise level, thereby reducing pilot-noise injection while retaining useful measurement information. We further design a conditional U-Net denoiser for complex-valued OFDM channel grids, where the real and imaginary components are represented as separate feature channels and downsampling is performed only along the subcarrier dimension. Simulations based on 5G NR tapped delay line (TDL) and clustered delay line (CDL) channel models show that DANCE achieves consistently lower normalized mean squared error (NMSE) than conventional estimators and diffusion-based posterior sampling methods under different signal-to-noise ratios, DMRS configurations, Doppler frequency shifts, and train-test distribution mismatches.

### [160] [Deep-Unfolded Wideband ISAC Beamforming for DMA Under Frequency-Selective Lorentzian Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03389)
*Abdolrasoul Sakhaei Gharagezlou,Pouya Mobaraki,Mehdi Monemi,Nhan T. Nguyen,Mehdi Rasti,Samad Ali,Matti Latva-aho*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究基于动态超表面天线（DMA）的宽带通感一体化（ISAC）系统，在频率选择性洛伦兹响应模型下，通过交替优化框架和深度展开投影梯度上升算法，联合优化通信和雷达性能。相比传统的频率平坦模型，所提方法提升约20%性能，并实现高达20倍收敛加速。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 建立频率选择性洛伦兹响应模型以准确刻画DMA元件的频率依赖行为；2) 提出基于投影梯度上升（PGA）的交替优化框架，推导数字波束赋形向量、谐振频率和阻尼因子的闭式梯度；3) 设计深度展开PGA架构，保留模型优化可解释性的同时学习超参数以加速收敛。

Conclusion: 本文验证了在宽带ISAC系统中采用频率选择性DMA模型的重要性，并证明了深度展开优化方法在保持可解释性的同时显著提升收敛效率。

Abstract: Integrated sensing and communications (ISAC), empowered by dynamic metasurface antennas (DMAs), has emerged as a promising paradigm for next-generation wireless networks. However, existing DMA-based designs commonly rely on the frequency-flat response model for DMA elements, which is accurate only in narrowband scenarios and can cause significant phase and magnitude mismatches in wideband and ultra-wideband systems. This paper investigates a DMA-based wideband ISAC system under a frequency-selective Lorentzian response model, which accurately captures the frequency-dependent behavior of DMA elements. We aim to jointly balance the aggregate signal-to-interference-plus-noise ratio (SINR) of communication users and the signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) of the radar target. To this end, we first develop an alternating optimization framework based on projected gradient ascent (PGA), deriving closed-form gradients of the objective function with respect to the digital beamforming vectors, resonance frequencies, and damping factors under the frequency-selective Lorentzian DMA model. We then propose an unfolded PGA architecture that preserves the interpretability of model-based optimization while learning key hyperparameters to accelerate convergence. Simulation results show that the frequency-selective Lorentzian model improves performance by approximately 20\% over its frequency-flat approximation. Moreover, deep-unfolded PGA achieves up to 20-fold faster convergence and improves the objective value by up to 7\% compared with PGA-based benchmarks.

### [161] [ATS-ToDMA: Adaptive Token Selection and Token-Domain Multiple Access for Cross-Modal Semantic Communications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03520)

TL;DR: 本文提出ATS-ToDMA框架，通过自适应令牌选择、令牌域多址接入和语义感知功率分配，解决语义通信中的令牌级多址接入和语义干扰问题，相比现有基准方法在语义吞吐量、解码准确率、干扰和功耗方面均取得显著提升。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语义通信框架忽视了令牌级多址接入以及同时传输的语义令牌之间的语义干扰问题，缺乏对令牌相似性导致语义干扰的建模与缓解机制。

Method: 提出ATS-ToDMA框架，包含：1）自适应令牌选择；2）基于语义信干噪比（SSINR）的干扰感知调度；3）语义感知功率分配；4）基于Transformer的调度器以缓解模态内和跨模态语义干扰；5）推导语义干扰和令牌占用的解析界，以及功率分配的闭式近似。

Abstract: Adaptive token processing has emerged as a promising approach for improving the efficiency of semantic communication systems. However, existing semantic communication frameworks largely overlook token-level multiple access and the impact of semantic interference among simultaneously transmitted semantic tokens. In this paper, we propose Adaptive Token Selection and Token-Domain Multiple Access (ATS-ToDMA), a novel cross-modal semantic communication framework that jointly performs semantic token selection, interference-aware scheduling, and semantic-aware power allocation. The proposed framework introduces a Semantic Signal-to-Interference-plus-Noise Ratio (SSINR) metric that captures the combined effects of channel impairments and semantic interference arising from token similarity. A transformer-based scheduler is developed to allocate selected semantic tokens across token-domain transmission slots while mitigating both intra-modal and cross-modal semantic interference. To characterize the behavior of the proposed system, analytical bounds on semantic interference and feasible token occupancy are derived, together with a closed-form approximation for semantic-aware power allocation. Simulation results demonstrate significant gains in semantic throughput and semantic decoding accuracy while reducing aggregate semantic interference and transmit power compared with OMA, Semantic NOMA, Random-TS, and Greedy ATS benchmarks.

### [162] [The Informational Cost of Structure: Representational Complexity in Networked Dynamical Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03608)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在回答"表示一个动力学系统需要多少信息"，并重新框架化网络表示选择问题——从追求普适表达能力转向信息成本和机制透明性的权衡。

Method: 基于算法信息论中的Kolmogorov复杂度定义表示复杂度；通过理论推导证明不同形式主义在无约束时的信息等价性；在约束条件下分析图与超图的信息偏好；由于Kolmogorov不可计算，辅以显式描述长度估计。

Result: 1) 表示复杂度为结构加规则模型提供了普遍下界；2) 任意规则下不同表示形式可等价地达到该下界；3) 科学约束（限制结构/规则类型）下出现图偏好、超图偏好或混合情形；4) 提供不可计算性的实用替代方案。

Abstract: How much information is required to represent a dynamical system in terms of an interaction structure and an evolution rule? We address this question using algorithmic information theory. We introduce Representational Complexity, the excess description length of a structure-plus-rule model relative to the shortest possible description of the dynamics itself. This intrinsic description defines a universal lower bound: no exact structural representation can be more concise. If arbitrary rules are allowed, graphs, hypergraphs, and other formalisms can all reach this bound by shifting information between structure and dynamics, so expressiveness alone cannot distinguish them. Meaningful differences arise only when scientific modeling restricts the admissible structures and rules. Within this setting, we identify conditions under which graph and hypergraph descriptions are informationally equivalent, and show how graph-preferred, hypergraph-preferred, and mixed regimes can emerge when those conditions are relaxed. Because Kolmogorov complexity is not computable, we complement the formal results with explicit description-length estimates. Our framework reframes the choice of network representation as a question of informational cost and mechanistic transparency rather than universal expressive power.

Abstract: Polar codes are proven to be capacity-achieving codes, being gradually practiced in wireless communications. However, their successive cancellation (SC) and successive cancellation list (SCL) decoding incur latency challenge especially for long codes. This paper proposes the generalized integrated interleaved (GII)-polar codes for block Rayleigh fading channels, yielding both reduced decoding latency and competent decoding performance. Under the GII paradigm, two consecutive polar codewords of length $N$ are virtually coupled through a nested codebook which has a lower dimension, capable of correcting more errors. The component polar codes are known as interleaves of a GII-polar code. If decoding of an interleave fails, it can be projected into the decoding of the nested one, enabling richer error patterns to be corrected by each interleave. Since decoding of the interleaves can be performed in parallel, GII-polar codes yield a reduced decoding latency over a single polar code of length $2N$. Our simulation results validate both the decoding latency and performance merits of the proposed coding scheme under block Rayleigh fading channel.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 1) 插入错误δ-分数下的列表译码容量精确值为(1+δ)(1-h(δ/(1+δ)))，对所有δ∈[0,1]成立；2) 马尔可夫链方法在删除错误下无法超越均匀随机编码；3) 删除错误下列表译码容量的上界在δ→0时渐近为1-h(δ)。

Abstract: Informally, the capacity of list-decoding in a given adversarial error model is the largest rate at which we can list-decode with list size polynomial in the block length. The capacity of list-decoding from insertions and deletions is a basic, yet poorly understood, aspect of coding against synchronization errors. For example, when dealing with a $δ>1/2$ fraction of insertions, the best known lower bounds give little more than the fact that the capacity is positive. Beyond that regime we also only have loose bounds, with the lower bounds stemming from the analysis of uniformly random codes.
  We make progress in our understanding of the limits of list-decoding binary codes from insertions and deletions. We show that the capacity of list-decoding from a $δ$-fraction of insertions is exactly \begin{equation*}
  (1+δ)\left(1-h\left(\fracδ{1+δ}\right)\right) \end{equation*} for all $δ\in[0,1]$, achieved with high probability by a code sampled according to a symmetric $2$-state Markov chain. Curiously, we complement this by showing that such an approach does not beat uniformly random coding in list-decoding from deletions. We also give an improved upper bound on the capacity of list-decoding from a $δ$-fraction of deletions, showing in particular that it behaves like $1-h(δ)$ when $δ\to 0$. This matches the asymptotic behavior of the capacity of the binary deletion channel for vanishing deletion probability.

*Kamila Szewczyk*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文改进了Shannon-Fano编码冗余度的上界，得到了依赖于最大源概率p₁的显式七段包络函数，首次给出了Fano码的p₁依赖冗余度界限，并在某些区间达到了精确上确界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Krajči等人2015年证明二元Shannon-Fano编码冗余度始终低于1比特的基础上，本文旨在进一步锐化该界限，得到一个依赖于最大源概率p₁的更紧致的冗余度上界。

Method: 不同于Huffman码的自底向上方法（具有兄弟性质），Fano树是自顶向下通过连续平衡分割构建的。本文利用Fano递归，通过最小修正的仿射势函数和"无埋葬引理"进行证明，每个标量不等式都归结为整数幂的比较。

Result: 得到了一个显式的七段包络函数R < f(p₁)。当p₁ ≥ 1/2时及在1/3以下的子区间上，该包络等于精确上确界；当p₁ < 1/2时，上界为R < 5/2 - (5/6)log₂5 ≈ 0.5651。

Conclusion: 这是第一个依赖于p₁的Fano码冗余度界限，通过比Huffman码更复杂的分析方法得到了精确的结果。

Abstract: Krajči, Liu, Mikeš, and Moser proved in 2015 that the redundancy of binary Shannon-Fano coding is always below one bit. We sharpen this to a bound depending on the largest source probability $p_1$: an explicit seven-piece envelope $R<f(p_1)$. The envelope equals the exact supremum of $R$ given $p_1$ for every $p_1\ge\tfrac12$ and on a subinterval below $\tfrac13$, and gives the cap $R<\tfrac52-\tfrac56\log_2 5=0.5651$ for $p_1<\tfrac12$. It is the first $p_1$-dependent redundancy bound for Fano codes. The method is more sophisticated than the approach typical for Huffman codes: Fano trees are built top-down by contiguous balanced splits and lack the sibling property. From the $R<1$ theorem the rest follows from the Fano recursion, through a min-corrected affine potential and a no-burial lemma. Every scalar inequality in the proof reduces to a comparison of integer powers.

</details>


### [172] [Orchestrating Communication, Computing, and Energy Transfer for Wireless-Powered 6G Closed-Loop Controls](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04225)
*Chengleyang Lei,Wei Feng,Yanmin Wang,Yunfei Chen,Xiaoyu Liu,Liuguo Yin,Ning Ge*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究了面向6G机器人控制任务的无线供能感传算控闭环系统，通过卫星射频能量传输为多闭环供能，并联合优化上下行功率、带宽、计算能力、时间及能量分配以最小化LQR代价，仿真验证了所提方案的性能优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 6G通信需支持机器人控制任务中感传算控闭环的长时间稳定运行，但设备电池容量有限限制了续航与控制效率，尤其在远程或灾后场景中问题更为突出。

Method: 提出无线供能SC3系统框架，卫星通过射频信号传输能量；以LQR代价为性能指标，建立最小化和LQR代价的优化问题；联合优化上下行发射功率、带宽、计算能力、通信/计算时间分配及WPT功率分配；将问题转化为更易解形式并设计迭代算法求解；针对单回路场景分析最优解性质。

Result: 仿真结果表明所提出的联合优化方案相比基准方案具有显著的性能增益。

Conclusion: 无线供能结合联合资源优化可有效提升SC3闭环控制性能，为6G工业自动化和应急响应等场景提供可持续的解决方案。

Abstract: Future sixth generation (6G) communications are expected to support robotic control tasks in applications such as industrial automation and emergency response, where sensors, computing units, and robots are interconnected via nervous system-like networks to form sensing-communication-computing-control (SC3) closed loops. However, the limited battery capacities of devices within these SC3 loops constrain operational duration and degrade control efficiency, particularly in remote or post-disaster scenarios. To address this challenge, wireless power transfer (WPT) can be leveraged to provide continuous energy supply for SC3 closed loops. In this paper, we investigate a wireless-powered SC3 system, where a satellite transfers energy via radio frequency (RF) signals to support the communication and computing processes of multiple SC3 closed loops. By accounting for the intricate coupling among computing, communication, and energy transfer, we propose a holistic design framework to enhance overall control performance. Specifically, we adopt the linear quadratic regulator (LQR) cost as the performance metric and formulate a sum LQR cost minimization problem. The uplink/downlink transmit power, bandwidth allocation, computing capability, communication/computing time allocation, and WPT power allocation are jointly optimized. We recast the problem into a more tractable form and develop an iterative algorithm to solve it. For the special case of a single loop, we further analyze the properties of optimal solutions in energy-limited scenarios to provide insights for practical parameter configuration. Simulation results demonstrate the performance gains of the proposed scheme.

</details>


### [173] [Rainbow Beamforming for Wideband LEO Satellite Communications: Principles, Applications, and Technical Challenges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04570)
*Juha Park,Hyungseok Ko,Haejung Kim,Namyoon Lee,Ian P. Roberts,H. Vincent Poor,Wonjae Shin*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种范式转变：将宽带LEO卫星通信中传统上被视为性能损害的波束斜射效应重新定义为一种有价值的频率-空间分集资源，并提出了彩虹波束赋形（Rainbow BF）技术，利用单条或少量射频链生成频率依赖波束，实现动态频率-空间波束分配，为6G LEO SATCOM提供增强的灵活性和可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上波束斜射效应被视为必须缓解的性能损伤，但作者认为在宽带LEO卫星系统中可将其重新利用为频率-空间分集的来源，以克服传统波束跳变等方案的延迟和吞吐量瓶颈。

Method: 彩虹波束赋形（Rainbow BF）：故意利用而非抑制波束斜射效应，使用单条或少量射频链生成频率依赖波束，使不同频率分量照射不同空间方向，实现动态频率-空间波束分配。

Result: 通过三个代表性应用场景展示了彩虹BF的优势：i) 大规模多址接入，克服传统波束跳变的延迟和吞吐量瓶颈；ii) 通感一体化，同时实现目标检测和数据传输；iii) 快速卫星捕获，降低搜索开销并提高链路可靠性。

Conclusion: 彩虹BF为宽带LEO SATCOM提供了一种全新的频率-空间分集利用范式，但面临关键实现挑战，需要进一步研究其在实际系统中的部署方案。

Abstract: Low Earth Orbit (LEO) satellite communications (SATCOM) has emerged as a key enabler of global connectivity for 6G networks. To overcome the significant path loss of space-to-ground links, high-gain directional beamforming (BF) is indispensable. As LEO systems evolve toward wider bandwidths to support data-intensive applications, however, they encounter a fundamental physical limitation known as the beam-squint effect, which induces frequency-dependent beam misalignment. Conventionally, the beam-squint effect has been treated as a critical performance impairment that must be mitigated. This article introduces a paradigm shift in wideband LEO satellite systems by redefining beam-squint as a valuable source of frequency-spatial diversity and presents the principles of rainbow BF. Rather than mitigating beam squint, rainbow BF deliberately exploits it to generate frequency-dependent beams, enabling different frequency components to illuminate distinct spatial directions using only a single or a small number of radio frequency chains. By supporting dynamic frequency-spatial beam allocation, rainbow BF offers enhanced flexibility and scalability for wideband LEO SATCOM. We further illustrate the benefits of rainbow BF through three representative LEO SATCOM applications: i) massive multiple access to overcome the latency and throughput bottlenecks of conventional beam hopping; ii) integrated sensing and communications for simultaneous target detection and data transmission; and iii) rapid satellite acquisition to reduce search overhead and improve link reliability. Finally, we discuss key implementation challenges and outline promising future research directions for rainbow BF in wideband LEO SATCOM.

</details>


### [174] [A Differentiable Covariance Calculus for Linear Gaussian Bayesian Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04578)
*Tadashi Wadayama*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种统一的协变微分计算框架，将线性高斯贝叶斯网络中的推理和估计任务简化为针对单一协方差矩阵的少量线性代数原语操作，并通过自动微分实现梯度计算，适用于任意向量值有向无环图及其参数化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有线性高斯贝叶斯网络（等价于线性高斯结构方程模型）中的推理和估计任务通常针对每个任务和每个拓扑结构单独推导和实现，缺乏统一的计算后端。本文旨在建立一个统一的微分协方差计算框架，使各种任务都能简化为在单一协方差矩阵上的线性代数原语操作。

Method: 以经典的可微映射K-recursion作为后端，构建统一的微分协方差计算框架。每个任务简化为对单一协方差矩阵的少量线性代数原语操作，通过自动微分在一次反向传播中返回所有梯度。该框架涵盖条件化、条件独立性检验（互信息）、含隐节点的最大似然估计、Slepian-Bangs Fisher信息量及其导出的局部可辨识性和Cramér-Rao可靠性。

Result: 在线性高斯状态空间模型和跳接（非链式）扩展模型上进行了验证，与Kalman递推、d-分割和Cramér-Rao界进行了对比。

Conclusion: 该统一的协变微分计算框架能有效处理任意向量值有向无环图上的各种推理和估计任务，为线性高斯贝叶斯网络提供了一种通用的计算范式。

Abstract: Linear Gaussian Bayesian networks, equivalently linear Gaussian structural equation models, recur across statistics, control, and communications; in the vector-valued setting that motivates this work, their nodes are vectors and their edges are matrices. Every quantity of interest is a function of sub-blocks of the joint covariance, which is itself a classical, differentiable map (the K-recursion) from the local edge and innovation parameters. Yet the resulting inference and estimation tasks are usually derived and implemented separately, per task and per topology. Taking this covariance chart as a single backend, we build on it a unified, differentiable covariance calculus in which each task reduces to a few linear-algebra primitives on the one covariance, and automatic differentiation returns every gradient in a single backward sweep, over arbitrary vector-valued directed acyclic graphs and parametrizations, including tied and structured ones. The calculus covers conditioning, conditional-independence testing through mutual information, maximum-likelihood estimation with hidden nodes, and the Slepian--Bangs Fisher information with the local identifiability and Cramér--Rao reliability it induces. It is validated on a linear Gaussian state-space model and a skip-connected (non-chain) extension against the Kalman recursions, d-separation, and the Cramér--Rao bound.

</details>

*V. R. Danilko,I. Yu. Mogilnykh,Ya. A. Tikhomolov*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用多种边界估计方法对5G NR标准中准循环LDPC码族的最小距离进行界定；提出基于循环模约减的早期终止技术来简化伴随式计算的复杂度。

Result: 高码率[9984,8448]码的最小距离范围在{8..14}，低码率[25344,8448]码的最小距离范围在{22..57}；提出的早期终止方法显著降低了解码器的伴随式计算复杂度。

Conclusion: 成功给出了5G NR标准中两种关键LDPC码的最小距离边界，并开发了一种有效的早期终止策略来降低解码复杂度，对5G LDPC解码器的实际实现具有重要意义。

Abstract: We propose several approaches for bounding the minim\-um distances of the family of quasi-cyclic LDPC codes in the 5G NR standard. In particular, we show that the high-rate [9984, 8448] and the low-rate [25344, 8448] BG1 5G LDPC codes have minimum distances in the ranges {8..14} and {22..57}, respectively. Also we propose a new early termination approach based on circulant modular reduction, which significantly lowers syndrome calculation complexity for the LDPC decoder.

### [176] [New Results on Limited Magnitude Error Correcting Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05026)
*Zhiyu Yuan,Tingting Chen,Rongquan Feng,Gennian Ge*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究有限幅度纠错码的存在性、构造与分类问题，重点探讨分裂集与群分裂的联系。在准完美分裂集方面建立了新的不存在性结果，并完成了奇异与非奇异情形下准完美$B[0,3](n)$分裂集的完全分类；通过凯莱图改进了最大$B[0,3](q)$集的规模下界；给出了完美$B[0,6](q)$分裂集和准完美$B[-4,4](2p)$分裂集的存在性判据；为完美突发纠错码构建了通用框架，证明了无限族$(k_1,k_2)$-有限幅度循环$b$突发纠错码的存在性。方法融合代数、组合与数论工具，推进了面向闪存及存储系统的编码理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 闪存等存储系统受限于物理特性，错误通常具有有限幅度特性，传统纠错码无法高效利用这一结构。为此需要专门设计有限幅度纠错码，分裂集与群分裂是构造此类码的核心工具，但相关理论仍不完善。

Method: 结合代数方法（群分裂理论）、组合方法（凯莱图、分类枚举）与数论方法（奇偶性分析、同余条件），对分裂集进行存在性、构造与分类研究。具体包括：利用群论建立分裂集的存在性判据；通过凯莱图分析推导下界；采用分类讨论完成完全分类。

Result: (1) 准完美$B[0,3](n)$分裂集在奇异与非奇异情形下的完全分类；(2) 最大$B[0,3](q)$集改进下界（q为素数）；(3) 完美$B[0,6](q)$与准完美$B[-4,4](2p)$的存在性判据；(4) 无限族$(k_1,k_2)$-有限幅度循环$b$突发纠错码的存在性（$k_1+k_2\le 4$，任意$b$）；(5) 一般参数$k_1,k_2$的充分存在条件。

Conclusion: 本文通过系统研究分裂集理论，显著推进了有限幅度纠错码的存在性判定与构造方法，为闪存及存储系统的编码设计提供了理论基础和实用工具。

Abstract: This paper investigates the existence, construction and classification of limited magnitude error-correcting codes, with a focus on splitter sets and their connections to group splittings. We establish new nonexistence results for quasi-perfect splitter sets and provide a complete classification of quasi-perfect $B[0,3](n)$ splitter sets in both singular and nonsingular cases. Furthermore, we derive improved lower bounds for the size of maximal $B[0,3](q)$ sets by investigating Cayley graphs, where $q$ is a prime. We also provide existence criteria for perfect $B[0,6](q)$ splitter sets and quasi-perfect $B[-4,4](2p)$ sets for prime $p$. For perfect burst-correcting codes, we develop a general construction framework, and prove the existence of infinite families of $(k_2,k_1)$-limited-magnitude cyclic $b$-burst-correcting codes for $k_1+k_2\le 4$ and arbitrary burst length $b$. We further provide sufficient existence conditions for general parameters $k_1$ and $k_2$. Our results combine algebraic, combinatorial, and number-theoretic methods to advance the understanding of codes tailored for flash memory and related storage systems.

</details>


### [177] [Security Analysis of RIS-Assisted Physical-Layer Authentication Over Multipath Channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05042)
*Linda Senigagliesi,Anna V. Guglielmi,Marco Baldi,Stefano Tomasin*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究了基于可重构智能表面（RIS）的物理层认证安全性。在Bob控制RIS的场景下，分析了多天线攻击者Trudy通过预编码欺骗认证的最优攻击策略，推导了信道不可区分条件，并指出在多径传播条件下单天线Trudy无法满足该条件，但在单径视距条件下可从不同位置成功冒充合法用户Alice。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在物理层认证中，攻击者可能利用多天线和预编码技术欺骗基于信道特征的认证机制。本文旨在分析引入RIS辅助后，系统在面对具备信道知识的攻击者时的安全脆弱性，特别是攻击者能否使Bob无法区分其与合法用户的信道估计。

Method: 首先假设Trudy已知所有信道矩阵，推导其最优攻击策略；然后分析Bob估计信道在Alice或Trudy发射时不可区分的条件；分别针对Trudy为单天线和多天线情况，以及多径传播和单径视距（LOS）场景进行理论分析。

Result: 1) 推导了Trudy的最优攻击策略；2) 多径条件下，单天线Trudy无法满足信道不可区分条件；3) 单径LOS条件下，单天线Trudy可从不同位置成功冒充Alice；4) 即使不可区分条件无法满足，仍对系统安全性进行了数值评估。

Conclusion: RIS辅助的物理层认证在视距传播条件下存在被攻击者从不同位置冒充的安全隐患，而在多径条件下对单天线攻击者具有天然防御能力。研究为RIS辅助物理层认证的安全性设计提供了理论依据。

Abstract: In physical layer authentication, verification of a user's identity is based on the characteristics of the transmission channel through which signals are delivered to the authenticator (Bob). In this paper, we assume that the signals received by Bob pass through a \ac{RIS} (controlled by Bob) and that the legitimate transmitter (Alice) is equipped with one antenna. Conversely, the attacker (Trudy) has multiple antennas and uses precoding to deceive Bob's verification. Assuming that Trudy knows all the channel matrices, we first derive her optimal attack strategy. Then, we analyse the conditions under which the channel estimated by Bob is indistinguishable when either Alice or Trudy is transmitting. When Trudy has a single antenna, we show that the indistinguishability condition cannot be met when the channels to the RIS are the result of propagation over multiple paths. For single-path line-of-sight (LOS) conditions, instead, Trudy can impersonate Alice although transmitting from a different position. We verify these results numerically and assess the security of the considered scenario, even when the indistinguishability conditions cannot be met.

### [178] [Epistemic Horizon Minority Games: When Abundance Reduces Strategic Value](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02765)
*Faruk Alpay,Levent Sarioglu*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文提出并正式化了“认知视野少数博弈”（EHMG）模型，研究当选项因公开可见而丧失战略价值这一机制。论文证明了固定认知势博弈约化、有限单调认知收敛、对数均场唯一性等理论性质，并通过实验和战略轨迹编码分析揭示了信息揭示与福利损失之间的复杂关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多战略情境中，选项的价值因其被公众关注而消失——一条路径、信号、押注或机会之所以有吸引力，正是因为只有少数人看到它。现有博弈模型未能充分形式化这种由认知可见性驱动的价值衰减机制。

Method: 构建认知视野少数博弈（EHMG）模型，在有限格点上定义具有有界观测视野、行动特定意识、欲望偏好的效用、随拥挤程度递减的收益的博弈结构。证明固定认知势博弈约化、有限单调认知收敛、对数均场唯一性等理论结果。通过实验模拟认知扫描、公共可见性冲击、认知约束下的Braess悖论等场景，使用多种轨迹编码方法（傅里叶摘要、递归图、Gramian图像等）进行战略结构识别。

Result: 证明了信息价格与总福利损失可以重合、分歧或推荐相反的信息披露政策；区分了私人揭示、公共共同揭示和相关群体揭示三种信号结构的不同均衡效应；通过反事实基线隔离了认知机制与普通完全认知拥堵的差异。

Conclusion: 战略价值因选项可见而下降这一机制可以通过EHMG模型被严格形式化，认知视野的有限性是战略互动中的核心因素，信息揭示的设计需要谨慎权衡其均衡效应。

Abstract: Strategic value can fall when an option becomes visible. A route, signal, bet, or opportunity may be attractive because few agents see it; public attention can erase the advantage it reveals. We formalize this mechanism as an epistemic-horizon minority game (EHMG), where agents have bounded observation horizons, action-specific awareness, desire-biased utilities, and payoffs that decline with crowding, and where the object is not a fixed congestion game with omitted actions but an awareness-transition game on a finite lattice. We prove fixed-awareness potential-game reduction, finite monotone awareness convergence, logit mean-field uniqueness under an explicit norm condition, non-reducibility from static count-based congestion games, and sensitivity bounds for nonlinear revelation. We separate the target price of information from aggregate welfare loss, showing that they can coincide, diverge, or recommend opposite disclosure policies, while modeling private revelation, public common revelation, and correlated group disclosure as distinct signal structures with different equilibrium effects. Experiments regenerate awareness sweeps, public visibility shocks, horizon-desire grids, information-constrained Braess examples, disclosure optimization, minimum harmful revelation, and counterfactual baselines isolating the epistemic mechanism from ordinary full-awareness congestion. Strategic trace encodings are evaluated as a controlled regime-recognition benchmark using raw trajectories, Fourier summaries, recurrence and Gramian images, image bundles, local-filter features, leakage probes, phase-scrambled controls, resolution and recurrence-threshold sweeps, spectral carriers, and IAAFT-matched null parameter-shift controls to test whether trace encodings recover strategic structure under robust nulls.

An agent may initially plan to complete a task, but later abandon it because, under non-exponential discounting, the perceived trade-off between immediate effort and delayed reward changes over time. This paper develops a tractable continuous-time model for analyzing and designing interventions for such agents in deadline-constrained progress-based tasks. In the model, an agent repeatedly chooses a future progress trajectory that minimizes perceived cost and then follows its infinitesimal initial direction. Although this leads to a continuous-time dynamic behavior defined through a variational problem, we show that the resulting trajectory admits a concise analytical representation under generalized hyperbolic discounting, a broad class of discount functions that includes exponential and hyperbolic discounting as special cases. Using this representation, we characterize when the agent completes the task, abandons it immediately, or exhibits time-inconsistent abandonment after making partial progress. We then study two intervention design problems: optimal goal setting and optimal reward scheduling. For goal setting, we derive optimal goals both when exploitative rewards are allowed and when they are prohibited, and we identify conditions under which exploitative rewards are ineffective. For reward scheduling, we show that, for a fixed number of stages, equal-length periods and equal rewards are optimal, and that finer reward splitting monotonically improves final progress up to a discount-independent limit. These results provide a continuous-time framework for intervention design for time-inconsistent agents and clarify how optimal interventions differ from those in existing discrete-time models.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Shapley值在数据集估值中具有组合定义带来的计算复杂性，现有方法缺乏对其在大规模数据源场景下行为特征的理论理解，亟需揭示其渐近结构和主导因素。

Abstract: We propose an asymptotic analysis of the Shapley value in a dataset valuation setting in which utilities are modeled as smooth functionals of empirical distributions via reproducing kernel Hilbert space (RKHS) mean embeddings. We prove that, despite its combinatorial definition, the Shapley value of a data source is asymptotically captured by a simple leading term. This term can be interpreted as the first-order contribution of a dataset relative to the surrounding data population. It also identifies the scale of the Shapley value as the number of data sources grows and provides a framework for analyzing existing Shapley value estimators. ### [182] [Random Serial Dictatorship is $\sqrt{2}$-Envy-Free](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03463)
*Frank Connor,Max Dupré la Tour,Louis-Roy Langevin,Vishnu V. Narayan,Ndiamé Ndiaye,Neil Rahman,Adrian Vetta*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文量化分析了随机序列独裁机制（RSD）及其扩展机制（随机轮循机制和迭代RSD机制）在房屋分配问题中的嫉妒率。主要结果是RSD的嫉妒率精确上界为√2，并对不同估值类别（加性、子模、XOS、子可加）给出了紧或近乎紧的边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管RSD机制因其简单性和精确刻画而成为经典研究主题，但其公平性的基本定量问题——即偏离无嫉妒程度的量化——长期未得到解决。RSD虽被视为事前公平，但实际上并非期望无嫉妒，因此需要量化其嫉妒程度。

Method: 定义嫉妒率为所有实例和代理对中，一个代理对另一个代理随机对象的期望效用与其自身随机对象期望效用之比的最大值。通过对RSD、随机轮循机制和迭代RSD机制在不同估值类别（加性、子模、XOS、子可加）下进行上下界分析。

Result: RSD的嫉妒率精确匹配为√2；随机轮循在加性估值下嫉妒率介于1.5和1.707之间；迭代RSD保持√2；子模估值下两种机制均有常数因子的上下界；XOS和子可加估值下嫉妒率无界。

Conclusion: 该研究首次为RSD及其自然推广近似无嫉妒的程度提供了紧或近乎紧的定量保证，完善了对此经典机制公平性的理解。

Abstract: We analyze the house allocation problem, in which a set of agents must be matched to a set of objects for which they have cardinal utilities. A central mechanism for this problem is random serial dictatorship (RSD), which has long served as a canonical subject of study due to its simplicity and the existence of exact characterizations by its properties. Despite this extensive understanding, a basic quantitative question about the fairness of this mechanism remains unresolved. Although RSD is often viewed as fair ex ante, surprisingly, it is not envy-free in expectation. We quantify its deviation from envy-freeness via the envy-ratio, which is the maximum over all instances and pairs of agents of the ratio between an agent's expected utility for another agent's random object and for its own random object. Prior work shows a factor-$\sqrt{2}\approx 1.414$ lower bound on the envy-ratio of RSD. Our headline result is a matching upper bound, showing that RSD is $\sqrt{2}$-envy-free in the house allocation problem.
  We further analyze the two natural extensions of RSD (the randomized round-robin mechanism and the iterated-RSD mechanism) to settings with unequal numbers of agents and objects and more general valuation classes. For additive valuations, this ratio increases to at least $1.5$ and at most $1.707$ for randomized round-robin, but remains exactly $\sqrt{2}$ for iterated-RSD. For submodular valuations, we prove constant-factor upper and lower bounds for both mechanisms, leaving only a small constant gap in both cases. For the more general classes of XOS and subadditive valuations, we present a tight analysis for both mechanisms, showing that the envy-ratio is unbounded in the number of agents. These results provide the first tight or nearly tight quantitative guarantees on the extent to which random serial dictatorship and its natural generalizations approximate envy-freeness.

</details>

Method: 理论推导与最优性证明。针对首轮投票，提出以候选人得票率的n/(n-1)次方为概率的选择规则；针对实例特定失真，推导了唯一最优规则的失真公式；针对top-k投票，推导了任意k≥2的 worst-case 失真公式，并改进了循环profile族的下界。

Conclusion: 所提规则是更简单且最优的替代方案，为随机社会选择的度量失真理论提供了完整刻画。

Abstract: We prove new upper and lower bounds on metric distortion for randomized social choice mechanisms. Under first-choice voting where each voter reports only their most preferred candidate, we show that selecting a candidate with probability proportional to the $\frac{n}{n-1}$-th power of their vote share achieves the optimal worst-case distortion of $3 - \frac{2}{n}$. This is a simpler single-rule alternative to prior work. We also study instance-specific metric distortion of first-choice mechanisms in terms of the vote vector $ν$. We show that there is a uniquely optimal rule achieving distortion $1 + \frac{2}{\sum_i \frac{ν_i}{1 - ν_i}}$. Finally, we extend our results to top-$k$ voting where each voter reports their $k$ nearest candidates. We derive a formula for the worst-case distortion for any $k\ge 2$. For the cyclic profile family this improves the previously best known $3 - \frac{2}{\lfloor \frac{n}{k} \rfloor}$ lower bound.

### [186] [Beyond Self-Resolution: Settlement Factorization for Robust Natural Language Mechanism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04382)
*Nicolas Della Penna*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文形式化了语言模型在付费建议场景中的"结算因子分解"框架，证明了报告与评估标签分离的必要性，并提出了基于幽灵分布重采样实现无影响参考的启示原理类比，量化了自身报告泄露ε对激励机制退化的影响边界。

Method: 提出结算因子分解（settlement factorization）形式化框架：报告固化→官方记录Z→外部化标签生成→付费。通过承诺的鬼分布（ghost distribution）重采样，建立启示原理类比的规范化形式。用总变差距离度量自身报告泄露ε，推导支付核灵敏度L下的真实边界退化上界2Lε，并证明该常数紧致。

Abstract: Language models increasingly mediate paid advice: agents submit open-ended forecasts, recommendations, plans, and evidence; a principal acts on the reports; and the mechanism later pays the contributors. Advice should influence the public decision, but no adviser should write the answer key used to evaluate it. We formalize the separation as settlement factorization: reports are hardened into official records, a public decision record Z may use all advice, and each paid adviser is scored against a label whose production is externalized from their own report, conditional on Z. The central result is an analogue of the revelation principle for this setting: resampling the paid report from a committed ghost distribution inside the settlement channel equips every mechanism with an influence-free reference within a factor of two of the best achievable, so factorization is a normal form, and own-report leakage varepsilon -- measured in total variation -- is an intrinsic invariant of any mechanism, identified behaviorally by worst-case incentive erosion. Settling a growing crowd on the shared decision record dilutes every margin exponentially in the informational redundancy, while a factorized leave-one-out label sustains a constant margin at unit stakes. Stakes outbid decision interests but never evaluator capture; randomized reference settlement makes integrity a threshold good priced per unit of total variation; and differential privacy of the evaluator in the paid report certifies varepsilon by construction.

*Yossi Azar,Itamar Biran,Amos Fiat*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究最小化版本的先知不等式（成本先知不等式）。在对抗顺序下，达到常数竞争比需要近乎线性的期望选择次数（Ω(n/ln n)）；而在先知秘书模型（随机顺序）下，仅需O(ln n)次期望选择即可实现常数竞争比。进一步，通过定义M（单个变量最小期望值与所有变量期望最小值之比），实现了O(min{ln ln M, ln n})次期望选择的常数竞争比算法，并证明该结果紧至对数因子。此外，确定性选择次数约束下任何常数竞争算法都需要n次选择。最后将该技术扩展到多单元变体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 最小化版本的先知不等式在经典最大化情形（简单阈值算法可达1/2竞争比）之外面临指数级下界的严峻挑战，亟需探索在允许多次选择（取最优）的松弛设定下如何平衡选择次数与竞争比。

Method: 论文针对不同顺序假设（对抗顺序、随机顺序/先知秘书模型）分别设计算法，通过分析M值（单个变量最小期望值与先知值之比）来刻画问题难度，并给出紧的下界证明。对于多单元变体，对i.i.d.变量扩展了相关技术。

Result: 对抗顺序下常数竞争比需要Ω(n/ln n)次期望选择；先知秘书模型下仅需O(ln n)次期望选择；进一步优化至O(min{ln ln M, ln n})次，且紧至低阶对数因子。确定性选择次数下任何常数竞争算法需n次选择。多单元i.i.d.变体同样实现了常数竞争比与小期望选择次数。

Conclusion: 证明了最小化先知不等式问题中，随机顺序（先知秘书模型）相较于对抗顺序能指数级降低所需的选择次数，给出了近乎紧的上下界，并成功将核心思想推广至多单元设定。

Abstract: We study the minimization counterpart of the classic prophet inequality, often termed the min prophet or cost prophet inequality. Unlike the maximization setting, where simple threshold algorithms achieve half of the prophet's value, the minimization setting is significantly harder, with an exponential lower bound even for i.i.d.\ variables.
  We study a multi-choice relaxation in which the algorithm may select multiple variables and gets to choose the best amongst them (the minimum amongst those selected). Our goal is to minimize the expected number of selections while achieving a constant competitive ratio. For adversarial order, we show that a constant competitive ratio requires a nearly linear number of choices in expectation, ergo, $Ω(n/\ln n)$. In contrast, we show that for the prophet secretary model (random order) one can attain constant competitiveness while requiring only an exponentially smaller expected number of choices i.e. $O(\ln n)$. We give a refined analysis and define $M$ to be the ratio of the minimum expected value of any single variable to the expected minimum value of all variables (the prophet's value) and present an algorithm that achieves a constant competitive ratio with $O(\min\{\ln \ln M, \ln n\})$ choices in expectation for the prophet secretary. We show that this is tight up to low order log factors even for the special case of the i.i.d. model. We also show that if we insist on a deterministic bound on the number of choices then every constant competitive algorithm requires $n$ choices. This holds even in the i.i.d.\ setting
  Finally, we consider a variant where both the algorithm and the adversary choose $r$ values and pay their sum, this is the minimization multi unit version. We extend our techniques to the multi-unit variant for i.i.d.\ variables, achieving a constant competitive ratio with a small expected number of choices.

</details>

### [188] [On the validity of using idealised sample geometries for interpreting mechanical tests of very soft tissues](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03079)
*Sajjad Arzemanzadeh,Karol Miller,Adam Wittek*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文研究了在软组织力学表征中使用理想化样本几何形状（标称立方体）对材料参数的影响，发现与基于MRI的真实几何形状相比，理想化几何形状始终低估剪切模量，差异在剪切模式下约10%，在轴向加载（特别是压缩）下高达48%，因此建议在逆向分析中使用实际测量的样本几何形状。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软组织力学表征常通过逆向分析将本构模型拟合到实验力-位移曲线，但大多数研究使用理想化（标称）样本几何形状，而实际样本因切割和安装偏差不可避免地偏离这些标称形状。这种几何简化对通过逆向分析确定的材料参数的影响尚未得到充分量化。

Method: 利用MRI重建标称立方体脑组织样本的真实几何形状；通过有限元方法分别模拟基于MRI的真实几何和理想化立方体几何下的拉伸、压缩和剪切测试；对比两种几何模型确定的剪切模量差异。

Result: 理想化几何形状始终产生更低的剪切模量；真实与理想几何间的剪切模量差异因加载模式而异：剪切模式下约10%，轴向加载下约48%，主要源于压缩响应；差异可归因于理想化几何模型无法准确表示接触相互作用和预测应变分布，尤其在压缩加载下。

Conclusion: 样本几何的理想化可能给非常软组织的力学表征引入系统性偏差；因此，在逆向分析中应使用实际测量的样本几何来识别本构模型及其参数。

Abstract: Mechanical characterisation of soft tissues often relies on inverse analysis of experimental data in which constitutive models are calibrated to match experimental force-displacement curves, yet the vast majority of such studies use idealised (nominal) sample geometries even though experimental samples unavoidably deviate from these nominal shapes because of imperfections in excision and mounting. The influence of these geometric simplifications on the material parameters determined through inverse analysis remains poorly quantified. We investigate the appropriateness of using idealised sample geometries in mechanical characterisation of brain tissue. Magnetic resonance imaging (MRI) was used to reconstruct the exact (real) geometry of each nominally cuboidal tissue sample. We determined a stress parameter (the shear modulus) by modelling, using the finite element method, tensile, compressive, and shear tests of brain tissue samples with both the MRI-based (real) and idealised cuboidal geometries, enabling a controlled comparison of geometry. Idealised geometries consistently yielded a lower stress parameter. The discrepancy in shear modulus between the real and idealised geometries varied across loading modes, averaging approximately 10% in shear and 48% under axial loading, predominantly arising from the compressive response. These discrepancies can be attributed to the inability of idealised-geometry models to accurately represent contact interactions and predict strain distributions, particularly under compressive loading. Idealisation of sample geometry may introduce systematic bias in the mechanical characterisation of very soft tissues; therefore, the actual measured sample geometry should be used in inverse analysis to identify constitutive models and their parameters.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前比特币研究广泛依赖链上指标，但这些指标分散于商业平台，定义不统一，且无法从原始区块链数据完全复现，阻碍了研究的透明性和可复制性。

Method: 从本地维护的Bitcoin Core全节点、持久化已花费输出索引器或对已有OBM序列进行确定性转换，构建每日时间序列数据；每个指标均附带开源Python代码、稳定标识符、明确定义、元数据、验证流程和解释性注意事项，并与现有公开指标进行对比。

Conclusion: 该数据集旨在支持货币经济学、金融经济学和区块链研究领域的透明实证研究、复制、教学和比较分析。

Abstract: Bitcoin research increasingly relies on on-chain indicators to study network activity, monetary issuance, transaction demand, miner incentives, coin-age behavior, and long-run monetary dynamics. However, many commonly used Bitcoin metrics are dispersed across commercial platforms, subject to heterogeneous definitions, or not fully reproducible from primary blockchain data. This manuscript introduces Open Bitcoin Metrics (OBM), a reproducible, full-node-derived dataset and reference guide for Bitcoin on-chain time series designed for economic and econometric research. The dataset provides documented daily series covering block production, block-space usage, transaction counts, supply, issuance, fees, miner revenue, mining difficulty, estimated hashrate, Bitcoin Days Destroyed, dormancy, liveliness, UTXO counts, spent output value, and related UTXO-age indicators. Metrics are reconstructed from a locally maintained Bitcoin Core full node, a persistent spent-output indexer, or deterministic transformations of previously generated OBM series. Each series is accompanied by open-source Python code, stable identifiers, explicit definitions, metadata, validation procedures, interpretive caveats, and comparisons with the closest publicly available metrics. The dataset is intended to support transparent empirical research, replication, teaching, and comparative analysis across monetary economics, financial economics, and blockchain studies.

### [190] [Uncertainty Quantification Study of a Re-entry Breakup](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03212)
*Tommy Williamson,Beatriz Jilete,Emma Stevenson,Stijn Lemmens,Massimiliano Vasile,Marco Fossati*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文通过刚体动力学模型模拟再入解体记录器（REBR4）在ATV3飞船再入过程中的行为，结合不确定量化分析，发现记录器在主解体事件前从货舱分离的可能性高于容器车辆高速旋转的假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大气再入过程中解体事件相关的严重不确定性需要更深入理解，利用解体记录器类传感器胶囊来获取数据的方法值得建模研究。

Method: 将解体记录器建模为经历高超声速气动热力学载荷及与解体容器碰撞动力学的刚体，对ATV3再入及REBR4进行确定性动力学探索，随后进行不确定量化分析。

Result: 不确定量化分析表明，记录器在主解体事件前从货舱分离的可能性高于容器车辆经历高旋转速率的替代假设。

Conclusion: 通过对初始航天器状态、REBR分离条件及航天器解体状态的不确定量化，推断出真实再入事件中记录器更可能提前脱离货舱而非容器高速旋转。

Abstract: The uncertainty associated with breakup events that occur during atmospheric re-entry is severe. Limited attempts to gain a better knowledge of this environment have included the use of breakup recorder-type sensor capsules that are designed to escape the demising debris cloud and survive in order to transmit data. This work models a breakup recorder undergoing this process as a rigid body experiencing hypersonic aerothermodynamic loads alongside collision dynamics with components of the demising container vehicle. The re-entry of the Edoardo Amaldi Automated Transfer Vehicle (ATV3) and the recorder placed on board, the Re-Entry Breakup Recorder 4 (REBR4) is studied in the present work. After a deterministic exploration of the nature of the dynamics of the problem, uncertainty quantification is performed to investigate the effects of initial spacecraft state, REBR detachment conditions and spacecraft fragmentation states. From this data, inferences about the nature of the real re-entry event indicate that detachment of the recorder from the cargo bay prior to main breakup events is more likely than the alternate hypothesis of the container vehicle experiencing high rotation rates.

### [191] [SPECTRA: A Physics-informed Digital Twin for Real-time Structural Anomaly Inference under Operational Variability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03446)
*Anshu Sharma,Basuraj Bhowmik*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: SPECTRA是一个物理信息驱动的特征压缩数字孪生框架，通过融合健康结构孪生模型、特征压缩动态表示、残差增强谱特征及持久决策规则，实现实时结构异常推断。在七个数值基准测试中，该方法能检测突变、渐变、非线性及阻尼相关损伤，且在无损伤工况下零持久误报，为基础设施数字孪生中的物理信息异常推理提供了可复现的测试路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 结构健康监测正从单纯的损伤检测转向面向老龄化及安全关键基础设施的实时决策支持，这要求监测方法能够区分真实结构变化与良性的环境及运营变异性，同时保持对工程师的可解释性。现有方法在分离环境/运营变异性与真实损伤方面仍存在挑战，且缺乏可解释的物理机制。

Method: SPECTRA框架结合了：(1) 健康结构孪生模型；(2) 特征压缩动态表示；(3) 全阶孪生新息；(4) 残差增强谱特征；(5) 核主成分分析；(6) 持久决策规则。核心思想是：结构异常不是仅从统计特征推断，而是从实测响应与物理信息健康孪生之间的差异（不一致性）来推断。

Result: 在七个数值基准测试（光滑Duffing型非线性漂移、突然刚度损失、渐近刚度退化、双线性呼吸刚度、环境与运营变异性混杂局部损伤、局部阻尼损失、纯运营变异性阴性对照）中，SPECTRA检测到突变、渐变、非线性和阻尼相关损伤机制，同时在仅运营变异性下避免了持久误报。持久决策规则在无损伤阶段给出零持久误报，损伤案例中有限检测延迟，无损伤阴性对照中零持久报警。

Conclusion: SPECTRA为在基础设施数字孪生部署前测试物理信息异常推理提供了可复现的路线，在区分真实损伤与环境/运营变异性方面表现出色，兼具检测灵敏度和低误报率。

Abstract: Structural health monitoring is moving from damage detection alone towards real-time decision support for ageing and safety-critical infrastructure. This shift requires monitoring methods that can separate true structural change from benign environmental and operational variability, while remaining interpretable to engineers. This paper presents SPECTRA, a physics-informed eigen-compressed digital twin framework for real-time structural anomaly inference. The framework combines a healthy structural twin, eigen-compressed dynamic representation, full-order twin innovation, residual-augmented spectral features, kernel principal component analysis, and a persistent decision rule. The central idea is that structural anomalies are inferred not from statistical features alone, but from disagreement between the measured response and a physics-informed healthy twin. The method is assessed through seven numerical benchmarks: smooth Duffing-type nonlinear drift, sudden stiffness loss, gradual stiffness degradation, bilinear breathing stiffness, environmental and operational variability-confounded local damage, local damping loss, and an operational-only negative-control case. The results show that SPECTRA detects abrupt, gradual, nonlinear and damping-related damage mechanisms, while avoiding persistent false alarms under operational variability alone. Across the accepted benchmark suite, the persistent decision rule gives zero pre-damage persistent false alarms, finite detection delay in damage cases, and zero persistent alarms in the no-damage negative-control case. The framework provides a reproducible route for testing physics-informed anomaly inference before deployment in infrastructure digital twins.

</details>


### [192] [Crypto-Microeconomics: The Distribution of Bitcoin Wealth Among Diverse Economic Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03646)
*Syed Azhar Hussain,Kashif Ahmad,Mubashir Husain Rehmani*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出“加密微观经济可观测性框架”，分析五类标记代理（服务、滥用、恶意软件、个人、良性）的比特币财富分布。发现财富高度集中：服务实体持有75.15%的比特币，滥用实体以3.53%的实体数量控制24.26%的比特币，各类别内部基尼系数接近1（如个人为0.9993），且这种“鲸鱼效应”在时间序列上持续存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多使用钱包余额、价格、哈希率等宏观指标分析比特币财富分布，缺乏从微观层面对不同类别经济代理（如服务商、恶意行为者、个人用户）之间财富差异的细粒度刻画。本文旨在填补这一空白，提出微观可观测性框架以揭示结构化不平等。

Method: 提出“加密微观经济可观测性框架”，将比特币经济代理标记为五类（Service, Abuse, Malware, Individuals, Benign）；采用描述性统计、不平等指标（如基尼系数）和纵向集中度指标进行分析。

Result: 服务实体持有最大份额（75.15%）；滥用实体以3.53%的实体数控制24.26%的BTC；个人、滥用和服务类别的基尼系数接近最大值（个人为0.9993）；时间序列分析表明不平等模式持续存在。

Conclusion: 比特币财富在标签化的经济代理中结构性地不均匀，集中在一小部分实体手中，呈现持续的“鲸鱼效应”。

Abstract: Bitcoin (BTC) wealth distribution is often studied with macro indicators like wallet balances, prices, network activity, fees, and hashrate. This letter proposes a "Crypto-Microeconomic Observability Framework" to examine micro-level Bitcoin wealth disparities across five labeled agent classes: Service, Abuse, Malware, Individuals, and Benign. Using descriptive, inequality, and longitudinal concentration metrics, we show that Bitcoin wealth is highly concentrated across major classes, consistent with a persistent "Whale-Effect". Service entities hold the largest share of observed BTC (75.15%), while Abuse controls a disproportionately large share relative to its entity count (24.26% of BTC vs. 3.53% of entities). Individuals, Abuse, and Service show near-maximal within-class inequality (e.g., Gini = 0.9993 for Individuals), and time-series analysis indicates these patterns persist. Overall, Bitcoin wealth among labeled economic agents remains structurally uneven and concentrated in a small subset of entities.

### [193] [The Objective Decides: When a Learned Dynamics Model Uses a Conserved Quantity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03728)
*Chih-Ting Liao,Xin Cao*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 线性探针从动力学模型激活中解码守恒量，并不能证明模型使用了该量。能量等不变量即使可完美解码（R²≈1），在下一状态预测中也是因果惰性的；只有当训练目标奖励该不变量时，该方向才变为因果承载的。部署因果性由输出代数决定，且能预测分布外准确率（r=+0.97），而可解码性对此无效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可解释性研究常将线性探针从模型激活中解码出守恒量作为模型"使用"该量的证据，作者质疑这一推理的有效性。

Method: 在力学、电路、偏微分方程系统以及1.58亿参数预训练PDE基础模型上，使用单步激活互换（activation interchange）测试因果性；通过更改输出代数结构翻转不变量的因果状态。

Result: 不变量可完美解码（R²≈1）但因果惰性（τ≈0）；改变训练目标使其奖励不变量后，因果性跃升至τ→+1；因果部署性可预测OOD准确率（r=+0.97），而可解码性完全无效。

Conclusion: 模型是否使用某知识应通过因果部署性而非可解码性来衡量；提供了低成本测量因果部署性的工具。

Abstract: A linear probe that recovers a conserved quantity from a learned dynamics model's activations is routinely read as evidence that the model uses that quantity. We show this inference is unsound. Across mechanical, circuit, and partial-differential-equation (PDE) systems, and on a 158M-parameter pretrained PDE foundation model, energy and other invariants are linearly decodable at $R^2 \approx 1$ yet causally inert on next-state prediction: overwriting the decoded direction with a donor state's value (single-step activation interchange) leaves the forward pass essentially unchanged (transfer-corr $τ\approx 0$). The same direction in the same representation becomes causally load-bearing ($τ\to +1$) the moment the training objective rewards the invariant, so deployment is a property of the objective, not of the representation or the probe. We further show that when an invariant is deployed is governed by a precise algebraic predicate (its relation to the prediction output), by flipping a single invariant from inert to load-bearing by changing only the output's algebra. Finally, the gap has teeth: across models that all decode the target at $R^2 = 1.00$, the deployment gap forecasts out-of-distribution (OOD) accuracy ($r = +0.97$) where decodability is blind. We argue that causal deployment, not decodability, is what interpretability should measure when the question is whether a model uses a piece of knowledge, and we give a cheap instrument for measuring it.

</details>


### [194] [Dynamic Image-Informed Selection of Biomechanical Tumor Growth Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04551)
*Abdullah Al Noman,Pratyush Kumar Singh,David A Hormuth,Danial Faghihi*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出一个序贯贝叶斯推断与动态模型选择框架，利用纵向小鼠MRI数据校准生物力学肿瘤生长模型中的空间可变参数。研究表明，力学耦合模型（尤其是超弹性模型）比单纯的反应-扩散模型具有更高的后验合理性，且随肿瘤进展力学效应日益重要，同时强调应对每个个体序贯评估本构假设而非预先固定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 胶质母细胞瘤的进展受肿瘤与脑组织之间力学相互作用的强烈影响，但有限变形力学及本构假设对个体化预测的改进程度尚不清楚。

Method: 建立了序贯贝叶斯推断与动态模型选择框架，通过纵向MRI数据校准空间变化的肿瘤扩散率、增殖率和组织刚度，并在每个成像时间点比较无力学耦合、线弹性耦合和超弹性耦合三种模型的后验合理性，实现逐个扫描的适应性模型选择。

Result: 力学耦合模型始终比无耦合模型更合理；线弹性和超弹性模型在肿瘤形态上相似，但在应力、变形和硬度场上有显著差异；超弹性模型在后期成像时间点常获得更高的后验合理性。

Conclusion: 力学耦合有利于基于影像的胶质瘤生长预测，本构假设应针对每个体序贯评估而非预先固定。

Abstract: Glioblastoma progression is strongly influenced by evolving mechanical interactions between the tumor and surrounding brain tissue. However, the extent to which finite-deformation mechanics and constitutive assumptions improve subject-specific prediction as tumor burden evolves remains unclear. We introduce a sequential Bayesian inference and dynamic model selection framework that assimilates longitudinal murine magnetic resonance imaging (MRI) data to calibrate spatially varying tumor diffusivity, proliferation rate, and tissue stiffness in biomechanical tumor growth models. Competing formulations were compared at each imaging time, including reaction-diffusion without mechanics and reaction-diffusion coupled to linear elasticity or hyperelastic mechanics, using posterior model plausibility to adapt model choice for individualized one-scan-ahead prediction as new MRI scans are acquired. Across the studied animals, mechanically coupled models were consistently more plausible than the uncoupled reaction-diffusion model, and the evolution of model plausibility indicated an increasing role of mass effect and stress-mediated feedback of tumor growth during progression. While linear and hyperelastic coupled tumor growth models often produced similar tumor morphology, they yield distinct stress, deformation, and inferred stiffness fields, with the hyperelastic formulation often receiving higher posterior plausibility at later imaging times. These results indicate that, within the present longitudinal murine dataset, mechanical coupling is favored for image-informed glioma growth prediction and that constitutive assumptions should be evaluated sequentially for each subject rather than fixed a priori.

</details>

*Minsuk Seo,Daniel A. Eisenberg,Jefferson Huang*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决数据稀疏环境下（如偏远地区）配水管网检测与维护决策困难的问题，这些地区无法获取管道级别的传感器数据，仅能依赖地表易获取的信息。

Method: 将问题建模为折扣马尔可夫决策过程，并与高保真水力仿真集成，无需管级传感即可捕捉潜在系统动态。

Result: 揭示了状态依赖的最优策略和管道间的异质故障特性（包括罕见但高影响的行为）；发现某些可观测系统状态与特定管道故障唯一对应，实现了虚拟感知。

Abstract: We develop a repair-oriented inspection and maintenance decision framework for water distribution networks. We formulate the problem as a discounted Markov decision process and integrate it with high-fidelity hydraulic simulation. The model captures latent system dynamics without requiring pipe-level sensing. The results reveal state-dependent optimal policies and heterogeneous failure characteristics across pipes, including rare but high-impact behaviors. We further show that certain observable system states uniquely correspond to specific pipe failures, enabling a form of virtual sensing. These findings demonstrate that system-level dynamics can support inspection planning and maintenance decisions under uncertainty in resource-constrained settings.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在泊松方程和平面应力弹性问题的数值实验中，伴随降阶模型快速收敛，性能优于原降阶模型，并能提供可靠的目标量估计。

Abstract: We introduce an adjoint-based reduced-order model framework for fast and accurate estimation of quantities of interest for many-query linear problems. The method builds a reduced-order model with respect to the adjoint problem, thus bypassing the solution of the primal problem and drastically reducing computational cost. It creates a surrogate model that is independent of the loading configurations. It enables fast evaluation across multiple load cases and the generation of virtual charts to support decision-making. Numerical experiments on the Poisson equation and a plane-stress elasticity problem demonstrate that the adjoint reduced-order model converges rapidly, outperforms its primal counterpart, and provides reliable estimates of the quantities of interest. Importantly, it is often more practical to parameterize a kernel function than an entire set of external loads, making the method generic and particularly suited for early-stage prototyping and design optimization.

### [197] [Modeling Fatigue-Induced Anisotropic Quasi-Brittle Damage Based on the Endurance Surface Concept](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04818)
*Klas Feike,Patrick Kurzeja,Kai Langenfeld,Jörn Mosler*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于耐久性表面概念的热力学一致的高周疲劳连续损伤框架，采用能量释放率作为驱动力，并通过微形态梯度增强实现网格客观性，成功应用于混凝土和钢材的疲劳模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有疲劳损伤模型在物理一致性、计算鲁棒性和多轴疲劳适用性方面存在不足，需要一种更合理的框架来模拟高周疲劳下的渐进损伤演化。

Method: 基于耐久性表面概念，以能量释放率作为热力学驱动力，损伤演化由驱动力与耐久性表面的距离决定；采用微形态梯度增强实现网格客观性，并引入各向异性损伤演化和微裂纹闭合-再打开效应。

Result: 成功标定了混凝土的单调解响应和低合金钢的高周疲劳行为；数值算例验证了单调破坏、应力-寿命行为和复杂多轴疲劳的模拟能力。

Conclusion: 该框架具有热力学一致性、梯度增强和计算鲁棒性，能够有效模拟高周疲劳驱动的损伤，尤其在多轴加载条件下各向异性退化的影响显著。

Abstract: This work proposes a novel continuum damage framework for fatigue based on the endurance-surface concept and uses the energy-release rate as the driving force. Damage evolution is governed by the distance of the thermodynamic driving force from the endurance surface. In contrast to classic failure surfaces, this allows damage to accumulate over many cycles even under constant-amplitude loading. The endurance surface therefore directly dictates the physical endurance limit of the material. To obtain mesh-objective results, the formulation is regularized by a micromorphic gradient enhancement. The incorporation of anisotropic damage evolution and the microcrack-closure-reopening effect extends the framework to multiaxial fatigue and loading-path-dependent degradation. The chosen prototype damage evolution fulfills three requirements: reasonable physics, computational robustness, and calibration flexibility.
  The model is successfully calibrated to both the monotonic response of plain concrete and to the high-cycle fatigue behavior of low-alloy steel. The numerical examples cover monotonic failure of an L-shaped concrete specimen, stress-life behavior under cyclic loading, and combined axial-torsional fatigue. These cases demonstrate how the proposed formulation applies to practical scenarios ranging from standard quasi-brittle fracture benchmarks to classical fatigue characterization and complex multiaxial damage evolution. The examples demonstrate that the formulation captures progressive degradation over many cycles and reproduces characteristic stress-life behavior. The influence of anisotropic degradation becomes especially relevant under multiaxial loading conditions during the near-failure phase. Overall, the approach provides a thermodynamically consistent, gradient-enhanced, and computationally robust framework for simulating fatigue-driven damage in the high-cycle regime.

</details>

This paper systematises the chain and taxonomises its documented failures. First, it systematises the supplier-quality evidence chain across the two dominant regimes, AIAG PPAP and VDA Volume 2 PPA, organised by artefact, producer, verifier, trigger, approval state, and retention. Second, it compiles a compendium of thirteen compliance-documentation failures made public 2012 to 2024, built strictly from the public record and each classified by evidentiary status (adjudicated, company-acknowledged, or alleged), with the Japanese certification cluster of 2016 to 2024 as centrepiece. Third, it builds a failure-mode taxonomy over the compendium, dimensioned by mechanism, lifecycle locus, driver, and detection path, shown exhaustive and discriminating over the case set. Fourth, it derives evidence architecture requirements mechanism by mechanism and sets an open-problems agenda. Across all thirteen cases, not one failure surfaced through the chain's own routine verification; the record indicts the verification layer, not only the evidence authors.
